<br/>
The Stables sits in a quiet, semi-rural residential area on the Central Coast of NSW. It’s so named due to its previous life as a shelter and stables for the horses that lived on the property. Such was the quality of the hardwood poles, frame and palings that every part of the original structure was re-used. With the timber sanded and brought back to its former glory a truly hidden gem began to emerge. Chris from Hooked on Carpentry, who poured his heart and soul into the project, said it was the nicest he’d ever completed!

The surrounding neighbourhood where we are located is a quiet and peaceful nature reserve , where on any given day a menagerie of wildlife can be seen, from koalas to water dragons. About a 5 min drive and 15 min bike ride, is the unique township of Byron Bay the world famous cosmopolitan melting pot where high end shopping meets dreadlocked surfers - there truly is something for everyone here, let alone the incredible stretches of golden beaches and stunning expanses of hinterland to explore...
<br/>
Even closer is a quiet beach trail, to a secluded stretch of Tallows beach which we can direct you too either by a 15 min walk or a 5 min bike ride.

Belle-Gordon is an elegant light filled garden studio 5 minutes walk from Blackheath Village
Beautiful Blackheath sits at the top of the Blue Mountains less than a 2hr drive from Sydney.  Stunning vistas surprise at the end of Govett’s Leap  and Evans Look Out Rds, both a short drive from the village. If gardens are your pleasure, then the Campbell Rhododendron Gardens on Bacchante St will not disappoint.  Oct-Nov is recommended as the best flowering time. Blackheath has a true 4 Season climate, warm Summers, stunning Autumn colours, chilly Winters with occasional snow falls and a glorious Spring with cherry blossoms and daffodils. Foodies & gourmets are catered for too with great cafes, restaurants, bakeries and local markets. Whether you are a hardened adventurer, or out for a pleasant stroll, the walks, tracks and canyons in Blackheath and surrounds, offer a variety of outdoor activity.

You’ll love the bungalow because of the comfy bed, the cosiness, waking up to the sounds and views of the the beautiful trees and laying in the bathtub under the canopy of the forest at night with some wine. Perfect for couples and solo adventurers.
None

Welcome to Bushies Love Shack. The naming of the love shack came about upon purchasing the property some 6 years ago. Fay's father, at the time 90 years of age, and his girlfriend, 91 years of age, automatically named it the Love Shack as they envisaged, once renovated, them sitting in bed, playing cards and taking in the view and so the name stuck. +++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
Beautiful, breathtaking views. We were so happy to stay in bed and enjoy the view or sit by the window with wine and cheese, that we didn’t want to leave for dinner! There are some great places to eat, not too far away. Looking forward to our next visit.
The best location we have ever stayed, a very special place.
Thank you Helen for an absolutely incredible getaway. Your home and hospitality including all those beautiful and thoughtful touches were very much appreciated
…
----------------------Neighbourhood-------------------------
<span class="_czm8crp">
With the Foxground Berry bypass now in operation the old Princes Hwy now Donovan Rd together with Foxground Rd have become the perfect cycling opportunity, offering both easy and challenging rides.
<br/>
If your arriving on a Sunday The Berry Country Fair is a good visit prior to checking in, held at the Berry showground between 8.30am – 2.30pm on the first Sunday of each month, Kiama Markets are held on the 3 Sunday of every month
<br/>
offering local produce, collectibles, books, art, crafts and plants.
<br/>
Berry and the surrounding area have several excellent restaurants including 
<br/>
South on Albany, Berry (one hat), Bangalay dining, Shoalhaven, The Blue Swimmer at Sea Haven, Gerroa, The Hungry Duck, Berry, Salmon &amp; Co Berry, Quattro pizza, Berry  Sourdough Bakery,Berry, The Hill, Gerringong. It is recommended you pre-book restaurants as the weekends are always very busy.
<br/>
Local wineries include Coolangatta Estate Winery, Crooked River Winery, the Silos, Two Figs Winery, Jasper Valley Wines, and Bundewallah Estate Winery.
<br/>
We are only 10 minutes to Werri beach in Gerringong and Seven Mile Beach National Park Gerroa.
<br/>
For golf enthusiasts, nearby courses include the Gerringong, Coolangatta Estate Winery (9 Holes), Shoalhaven Heads, Kangaroo Valley, Nowra.
<br/>
Further afield you will find Arthur Boyd's Bundanon on the of the Shoalhaven River, and the beautiful beaches and national parks of Jervis Bay. it takes about an hour to drive to the southern highlands via Kangaroo Valley Then there are many varied fabulous walks throughout the region
<br/>
If you have a specific request or would like further advice or suggestions for activities during your stay, please let us know and we will do everything we can to assist.

----------------------introduction-------------------------
In the Byron Bay Hinterland, 25 minutes from Byron, wake up on top of a mountain to the sunrise & one of the most extraordinary locations in the Shire. Looking over the valley & the Pacific Ocean, Kinabalu is essentially a Private Conservation Park. Surrounded by the Inner Pocket Nature Reserve henceforth one of our main goals are the conservation, rejuvenation and repair of the rainforests of the estate. Come and  look and I might get to tell you a story of the ancient forests of Gondwana.
The area is loved for its lush green growth, abundant water with its many waterfalls, and picturesque scenery. Not to mention it's fabulous beaches. Please take note that we are in the middle of the jungle. Inner Pocket Nature Sanctuary is filled with the most extraordinary array of birds, animals & insects. This is on the middle of virgin wild nature. For some this could be frightening. So be prepared. Bring walking shoes, insect repellent, a torch & a raincoat. You never know!
----------------------amentities-------------------------
Kitchen
Hot tub
Free parking on premises

Our neighbourhood is quiet and residential, made up of local and holiday houses.Being at the end of a Cul de sac, there is little traffic in or out.  Having direct access to the Ocean and the River, we are spoiled with the pretty sounds of abundant bird life around the house.

----------------------introduction-------------------------
Elphin is on a steep private gully and faces north and east, with its beautiful new interiors, stylish antique pieces meets rustic sheik, large windows and views in all directions, a great deck and a comfy bed that guests have named “the cloud”. The gulley is full of terraced gardens and native fern bushland and sits above Leura Creek which feeds into the great Bridal Veil Falls. There is a bedroom with eating table and a full new kitchen, super creative bathroom and private deck.
Elphin is in the centre of the Blue Mountains exactly half way between the two major villages - Leura and Katoomba (15 mins walk to Leura and 20 mins to Katoomba). Our favourite places for walking with the pooch are the Charles Darwin Walk, Wentworth Falls Lake and the abandoned (but beautifully mown) Katoomba golf course with its century old, established gardens and magnificent trees.

Kitchen
Pay TV

Designed to represent the Australian settler’s cottage, unique and cozy, the fully fenced verandah overlooks the water. ----------------------introduction-------------------------
'The Dairy' was one of the original dairy milking sheds in Upper Kangaroo River. This cottage has been lovingly restored and creatively transformed into luxury accommodation using reclaimed and recycled materials. A luxurious eco-haven for a peaceful escape from the everyday world! The three sets of French doors, which used to allow three cows in to be milked at once, now allow the living area to be opened to the alfresco dining area which is covered by an old wisteria vine.
The dairy is located on a quiet rural road, about 6 km from the main village of Kangaroo Valley. The Dairy is close enough to go in for a nice meal at one of the local restaurants, but far enough away to feel you have escaped from the hustle and bustle of life! Surrounded by farmland and bush - a peaceful stay for all travellers.

Kitchen
Free parking on premises

None

Such a perfect little retreat. We adored waking up to the amazing views and we're more than cosy and comfortable! Would definitely return!
----------------------Neighbourhood-------------------------
<span class="_czm8crp">
The Pambula rivermouth is often referred to as the jewel of the far south coast. Pristine clear waters, amazing walking tracks, and peace and serenity. When you seek other adventures it’s a short bike ride or drive to the many restaurants, shops and cafes in Pambula and Merimbula. Fresh local oysters and oyster tours are also readily available!
<br/>
Kangaroos, wallabies and echidnas are common place in our gardens here, not to mention a wide variety of birdlife. Whales and dolphins are also often to be spotted here, on our morning and afternoon strolls we often see them surfing and playing metres away from us. 
<br/>
There’s very little car traffic on our street and indeed Pambula Beach is tucked away from any thoroughfare so it remains undeveloped by retail or too many people passing through. 
<br/>
One takeaway shop and small convenience store a few mins walk away, just like the old days!!

You have found one of the best food locations in Sydney to stay during your visit. Surrounded by busy cafes and popular restaurants, Potts Point is a vibrant "inner city village" that is walking distance away from city centre, Sydney Harbour, Opera House, NSW Art Gallery, Australian Museum, beautiful parks and excellent public transport is minutes away.
Rich with history, culture and sophistication, Potts Point is an ideal place to stay or visit for those who want to enjoy the picturesque surroundings of a bygone era and still be close to everything Sydney has to offer.

<span class="_czm8crp">
The neighbourhood is quiet as house is in a residential street. As the bay is quite small, there are never large crowds using the beach. The golf course &amp; club are very picturesque being on the ocean front. The ocean pool is very popular with guests and with ourselves as it is 5 minutes walk so no need to take anything with you but your towel, keys and sunscreen.
<br/>
 Nearest eating and drinking venues are the Leagues club which also provides reasonably priced and varied meals. The golf club is more expensive but still good value. There is also a Chinese restaurant and fast food places within a 10 minute walk and some excellent cafés especially the Heritage and Beach Cafés. La Perouse, Little Bay, Yarra Bay and Maroubra are 10 minutes drive away and have a good selection of cuisines.

…
----------------------Neighbourhood-------------------------
<span class="_czm8crp">
Smiths Lake is a quiet holiday village situated approx 250km north of Sydney and 25km south of Forster.  The lake is connected to our beautiful Cellito Beach.  You can get to the beach by kayak (from the house) or by car (5min drive) or you can have a swim in the lake.  In the village you will find a small general store, bottle shop, cafe, a butcher, a bakery, hairdresser/beautician and the famous Frothy Coffee cafe situated overwater on the lake front (with boat/kayak hire facilities).  There is also a small playground area near the cafe.  Pacific Palms Bowling Club has a nice restaurant and live entertainment on weekends.
<br/>
Within 10min drive you will also have access to Blueys Beach, Boomerang Beach, Elizabeth Beach in the Pacific Palms area.  Perfect surfing conditions on every beach (weather permitting). There are more shops, cafes, restaurants etc there.   Forster/Tuncurry is only about 20min drive away – you will find there large shopping centres, more beautiful beaches, pools, tennis courts, cinemas and more other holiday attractions.

Suffolk Park is a vibrant community 5km south of Byron Bay set on beautiful unspoilt Tallow Beach. There is a great pub, a couple of restaurants and great café/bakery as well as supermarket, chemist and gym just 250m walk from our property. To get into Byron it's a flat 5km bike ride or 5 minute drive.  Other options are to take a  bushwalk through beautiful aboriginal reserve bushland opposite the property to a hidden tea tree lake and unspoilt Tallows and Broken Head beaches.  The nearest beach is only 600m walk from our property.

Suffolk Park is a vibrant community 5km south of Byron Bay set on beautiful unspoilt Tallow Beach. There is a great pub, a couple of restaurants and great café/bakery as well as supermarket, chemist and gym just 250m walk from our property. To get into Byron it's a flat 5km bike ride or 5 minute drive.  Other options are to take a  bushwalk through beautiful aboriginal reserve bushland opposite the property to a hidden tea tree lake and unspoilt Tallows and Broken Head beaches.  The nearest beach is only 600m walk from our property.

Traditional style spacious Sioux tipi with hinterland views. A unique glamping experience - wooden floors, kitchen with gas cooker & running water, comfy queen bed & outdoor bathroom. Close to beaches, Byron Bay & festivals.
Tandys Lane is a lush green location with a rural farm vibe as most properties are acreage with cows, chickens, horses, orchards etc. Easy & quick access to Brunswick, Mullumbimby & Byron Bay as we are close to the Highway.

Thanks for writing us a great review Michael. It always makes us happy when guests enjoy their stay.
----------------------Neighbourhood-------------------------
<span class="_czm8crp">
Our property is located in the small rural community of Dunmore. Located on the western side of the Princes Hwy. The eastern property boundary is adjacent to the highway. The western boundary is 45 minute relaxed walk from the cottage. 
<br/>
Kiama is 15 minute drive to the south.
<br/>
Shellharbour is 7 minute drive to the east.
<br/>
Killalea, The farm beach is 7 minute drive to the east.
<br/>
Minnamurra rainforest is 25 minute drive to the south west.
<br/>
Jamberoo Recreation Park is 20 minute drive to the west.

You might want to pause at this listing--you've just discovered the most desirable little cottage in Daylesford! Circa 1860, Headland is one of Daylesford's originals--cosy, beautifully styled & oozing authentic appeal. So special & quaint, even the famous 'Urban List' has discovered her charms & placed this little beauty 3rd in its list of "Everything Worth Eating, Seeing And Doing in Daylesford". We're very chuffed & would love you to discover this bijou, little timber cottage for yourselves!
Headland was once part of a large farming estate & housed one of its many working families. As such, it is surrounded by much grander family homes which only further serves to enhance its quaint colonial appeal.

Kilfeacle is a pretty unique place. The forest at the edge of the paddocks is a continuity of the very special Budawang Wilderness Area, home to endangered species of plants and animals. On a clear night  the sky is filled with stars, as there is no light at all to be seen to our north and west. You might hear frogs, owls, bats and boobooks, but that is about it. And yet, if you feel like a treat, Milton is only an 8km drive away with the famous Milton Theatre, well-known cafes and award-winning restaurants and cafes (like Tallwood, Native and Milkhaus - you have to go!). And we're just 3 hours drive from Sydney. Come and see!
----------------------amentities-------------------------
Wi-Fi
Kitchen
Free parking on premises

----------------------introduction-------------------------
Humble renovated 3 bedroom 1960's beach house in the heart of Cabarita Beach.
Cabarita Beach is a beautiful slow beach side town. It is laid-back but there is enough developing in surrounding areas to keep you busy. 
----------------------amentities-------------------------
Wi-Fi
Kitchen
Free parking on premises
